## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kafka Connect REST API v1 to v2 Migration

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the Kafka Connect REST API: the v1 connector resource handlers, the v2 connector resource handlers, and the version routing logic. Identify what changed between v1 and v2 in the task status and error response schemas.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [

  ],

    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

The API has evolved in-place within a single handler class.\n\n---\n\n### Complete Inventory of Java Source Files Implementing the Kafka Connect REST API\n\n#### Public REST Resource Handlers\n\n**`connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/ConnectorsResource.java`**\n- `@Path(\"/connectors\")` \u2014 the sole public connector handler\n- Handlers\n\n**`connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/InternalClusterResource.java`**\n- Abstract base class for worker-to-worker communication\n- Defines: `POST `@Path(\"/connectors\")` \u2014 concrete subclass of `InternalClusterResource` for standard Connect workers\n- Provides the `Herder` instance for intra-cluster requests\n\n**`connect/mirror/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/mirror/rest/resources/InternalMirrorResource.java`**\n- `@Path(\"/{source}/{target}/connectors\")` \u2014 concrete subclass of `InternalClusterResource` for MirrorMaker 2\n- Routes intra-cluster requests to the correct `Herder` based on source/target cluster pair\n\n#### Admin Resource\n\n**`connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/LoggingResource.java`**\n- Admin-port-only resource for dynamic log level management\n\n#### Server Setup and \"Version Routing\"\n\n**`connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/RestServer.java`**\n- Abstract Jetty-based server base class\n- Implements the **public vs. admin port split** (the only \"routing\" in the system): regular resources go to the main listener; admin resources go to a separate admin listener (virtual-host routed via `@Admin` connector name)\n- Registers `ConnectExceptionMapper` globally for all resources\n\n**`connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/ConnectRestServer.java`**\n- Concrete `RestServer` for standard Connect `LoggingResource`\n\n**`connect/mirror/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/mirror/rest/MirrorRestServer.java`**\n- Concrete `RestServer` for MirrorMaker 2 (internal-only, no public endpoints)\n- Regular resources: `InternalMirrorResource` only\n\n#### Error Response Infrastructure\n\n**`connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ErrorMessage.java`**\n- The single, unified error response schema (no v1/v2 split)\n\n**`connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/errors/ConnectRestException.java`**\n- Exception type carrying both `statusCode` (HTTP) and `errorCode` (application-level, can differ)\n\n**`connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/errors/ConnectExceptionMapper.java`**\n- JAX-RS `ExceptionMapper<Exception>` \u2014 converts all uncaught exceptions to `ErrorMessage` JSON\n\n#### Task Status Schema\n\n**`connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ConnectorStateInfo.java`**\n- REST response schema for `GET /connectors/{connector}/status` and `GET /connectors/{connector}/tasks/{task}/status`\n\n**`connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/KafkaStatusBackingStore.java`**\n- Internal Kafka-topic schema (`STATUS_SCHEMA_V0`) for persisting status \u2014 not the REST API schema\n\n---\n\n### Schema Specifications\n\n#### Task Status REST Response (`ConnectorStateInfo.TaskState`)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"id\":        <int>,\n  \"state\":     <string>,\n  \"worker_id\": <string>,\n  \"trace\":     <string, omitted when null/empty>,\n  \"version\":   <string, omitted when null or \"unknown\">\n}\n```\n\nThe `version` field (connector/task plugin version) is conditionally serialized via `@JsonInclude(CUSTOM, valueFilter = PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter.class)` \u2014 it is suppressed when the value is `null` or the sentinel string `\"unknown\"`. The `trace` field uses `@JsonInclude(NON_EMPTY)`.\n\nThe full connector status response (`ConnectorStateInfo`) wraps this:\n```json\n{\n  \"name\":      <string>,\n  \"type\":      <string>,\n  \"connector\": { \"state\": ..., \"worker_id\": ..., \"trace\": ..., \"version\": ... },\n  \"tasks\":     [ { \"id\": ..., \"state\": ..., \"worker_id\": ..., \"trace\": ..., \"version\": ... }, ... ]\n}\n```\n\nNote: `ConnectorState` uses `@JsonProperty(\"msg\")` for its constructor parameter but the field is stored as `trace` in `AbstractState` \u2014 both `ConnectorState` and `TaskState` accept `msg` on deserialization but serialize as `trace`.\n\n#### Error Response (`ErrorMessage`)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"error_code\": <int>,\n  \"message\":    <string>\n}\n```\n\n`ConnectExceptionMapper` produces this for every exception:\n- `ConnectRestException` \u2192 uses its own `statusCode` (HTTP) and `errorCode` (application-level, may differ, e.g., HTTP 409 with custom app code)\n- `NotFoundException` (Connect or JAX-RS) \u2192 HTTP 404, `error_code: 404`\n- `AlreadyExistsException` \u2192 HTTP 409, `error_code: 409`\n- `WebApplicationException` \u2192 uses embedded HTTP status for both HTTP status and `error_code`\n- All other exceptions \u2192 HTTP 500, `error_code: 500`\n\n#### Internal Kafka Topic Status Schema (`KafkaStatusBackingStore.STATUS_SCHEMA_V0`)\n\nThis is the **only versioned schema** in the codebase (named `_V0`). It is the Connect data schema used to serialize status records into the internal `connect-status` Kafka topic \u2014 it is **not** the REST API response schema:\n\n```\nStruct {\n  state:      STRING  (required)\n  trace:      STRING  (optional)\n  worker_id:  STRING  (required)\n  generation: INT32   (required)\n  version:    STRING  (optional)\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Why There Are No v1/v2 REST Handlers\n\nThe Kafka Connect REST API has always been unversioned at the URL level. New capabilities (e.g., `version` field in task status added for plugin versioning, `offsets` endpoints, `stop` endpoint, `PATCH /config`) were added **backward-compatibly in-place** to `ConnectorsResource` rather than through a versioned split. The `_V0` suffix in `STATUS_SCHEMA_V0` refers to the internal Kafka topic wire format schema version, not the REST API version."
